                        "content": "Biodiesel is a clean burning substitute for petroleum based diesel fuel. Biodiesel is made of vegetable oil. <br \/>\nTo make or manufacture Biodiesel, you must first start with raw materials. The raw materials needed in the production of Biodiesel are a small amount of methanol and a ready supply of vegetable product. One of the most common vegetables used in the production of Biodiesel is corn, although depending on the geographic location of the manufacturing facility many other plants are used as well (rapeseed, soybeans, flaxseed, etc.). The first step is to use the raw vegetable product to make vegetable oil. Vegetable oil by itself will not be what you need to power a car, from here it has to be processed into Biodiesel. <br \/>\nThe process for converting vegetable oil into Biodiesel is sometimes called ester interchange. To complete this process the vegetable oil has to be combined with a smaller amount of methanol and then put in the presence of a small quantity of an alkaline catalyst (for example, 5% to 1% sodium hydroxide). Vegetable oil is made up of so-called triglycerides, which is a compound of the trivalent alcohol glycerin with three fatty acids. The goal of ester interchange is to separate the glycerin molecule from the three fatty acids and replace it with three methanol molecules. This process then yields roughly 90% Biodiesel and 10% of a glycerin byproduct. The glycerin byproduct can be used in a number of other chemical processes for different industries.<br \/><br \/><br \/><br \/>\nada yg bisa bantuin bikinin10 s0al dari teks ini ",

Biodiesel is made of vegetable oil.<br \/>To make or manufacture Biodiesel, you must first start with raw materials. The raw materials needed in the production of Biodiesel are a small amount of methanol and a ready supply of vegetable product. One of the most common vegetables used in the production of Biodiesel is corn, although depending on the geographic location of the manufacturing facility many other plants are used as well (rapeseed, soybeans, flaxseed, etc.). The first step is to use the raw vegetable product to make vegetable oil. Vegetable oil by itself will not be what you need to power a car, from here it has to be processed into Biodiesel.<br \/>The process for converting vegetable oil into Biodiesel is sometimes called ester interchange. To complete this process the vegetable oil has to be combined with a smaller amount of methanol and then put in the presence of a small quantity of an alkaline catalyst (for example, 5% to 1% sodium hydroxide). Vegetable oil is made up of so-called triglycerides, which is a compound of the trivalent alcohol glycerin with three fatty acids. The goal of ester interchange is to separate the glycerin molecule from the three fatty acids and replace it with three methanol molecules. This process then yields roughly 90% Biodiesel and 10% of a glycerin byproduct. The glycerin byproduct can be used in a number of other chemical processes for different industries.<br \/><br \/>Semoga ada yang bisa membantu<br \/>Terimakasih sebelum nya :)",

One\nimportant aspect of the controversy is\nwhether a woman should be permitted\nby law to have an abortion and, if so,\nunder what circumstances. Another\nis whether, and to what extent laws\nshould protect the unborn. People who\nwish to legally limit or forbid abortions\ndescribe themselves as pro\u2013life. Those\nwho believe that a woman should have\nthe right to have an abortion may refer\nto themselves as pro\u2013choice.\nArguments against abortion are\nbased on the belief that an abortion\nis the unjusti ed killing of an unborn\nchild. Most people who oppose abortion\nbelieve that human life begins when\na sperm fertilises an egg. Another\nargument against abortion is that laws\nallowing it on demand will increase\nirresponsible pregnancies and lead to\ndisrespect for human life. The Roman\nCatholic Church is a chief opponent\nof abortion. Conservative branches of\nother religions also oppose abortion.\nMany people approve of abortion\nunder certain circumstance. Some\napprove of abortion if a woman\u2019s life or\nhealth is endangered by her pregnancy.\nOthers recommend abortion when\nthere is danger that the child will be\nborn with a serious mental or physical\ndefect. They also approve of abortion\nwhen pregnancy has resulted from <em>rape<\/em>\nor incest.\nMany people who think that a\nwoman should have the right to choose\nto have an abortion distinguish between\nhuman life and personhood. They\nargue that personhood implies both\nthe capacity for self-conscious thought\nand acceptance as a member of a social\ncommunity. These people believe a fetus\nis not a person and is thus not entitled to\nrights normally given to a person. Such\npro\u2013choice supporters agree with the\nview that birth represents the beginning\nof personhood.\nAnother pro\u2013choice argument is\nthat legalising abortions has eliminated\nmany illegal abortions performed by\nunskilled practitioners under unsanitary\nconditions. These abortions often cause\ndeaths and permanent reproductive\ninjuries. Abortion on demand also\nprevents many unwanted births and\nmay thus be a factor in lowering infant\nand child abuse, neglect, and death\nrates. Also some argue that women\nshould not have to bear unwanted\nchildren in a world with a growing\npopulation and diminishing natural\nresources.\nAs a result of this controversy,\nabortion laws vary from country to\ncountry. In Russia, where abortion has\nbeen legal since 1920, it is allowed up to\nabout the fourth month of pregnancy,\npurely by request, and is commonly\nused as a method of birth control. In\nsome countries, such as the Philippines,\nIndonesia, and Bangladesh, abortion\nis only allowed when pregnancy\nthreatens the mother\u2019s life. South Africa,\nNew Zealand, and Hong Kong allow\nabortion when the fetus is severely\ndamaged. In the Republic of Ireland,\nthe operation may only be performed\nwhen either the mother\u2019s or baby\u2019s life\nis in danger.\nTaken from The World Book Encyclopedia, 2007\nWorks in pairs.
